[2023-12-15 17:25:14] @w:matrixtcFJHPDblmt2rg.network: # Check corp network info

## TOTAL SERVERS

```
powershell -c "$i=0;$D=[System.DirectoryServices.ActiveDirectory.Domain]::GetCurrentDomain();$L='LDAP://'.$D;$D = [ADSI]$L;$Date = $((Get-Date).AddDays(-90).ToFileTime());$str = '(&(objectcategory=computer)(operatingSystem=*serv*)(|(lastlogon>='+$Date+')(lastlogontimestamp>='+$Date+')))';$s = [adsisearcher]$str;$s.searchRoot = $L.$D.distinguishedName;$s.PropertiesToLoad.Add('cn') > $Null;$s.PropertiesToLoad.Add('operatingsystem') > $Null;$s.PropertiesToLoad.Add('description') > $Null;$s.PropertiesToLoad.Add('distinguishedName') > $Null;Foreach ($CA in $s.FindAll()){;Write-Host $CA.Properties.Item('cn'); $CA.Properties.Item('operatingsystem'); $CA.Properties.Item('description'); $CA.Properties.Item('distinguishedName'); $i++;}; Write-host Total servers: $i"
```

## TOTAL COMPUTERS

```
powershell -c "$D=[System.DirectoryServices.ActiveDirectory.Domain]::GetCurrentDomain();$L='LDAP://'.$D;$D = [ADSI]$L;$Date = $((Get-Date).AddDays(-90).ToFileTime());$str = '(&(objectcategory=computer)(|(lastlogon>='+$Date+')(lastlogontimestamp>='+$Date+')))';$s = [adsisearcher]$str;$s.searchRoot = $L.$D.distinguishedName;$s.PageSize = 10000;$s.PropertiesToLoad.Add('cn') > $Null;Foreach ($CA in $s.FindAll()){;$i++;}; Write-Output Total computers: $i"
```

## TRUSTS

```
nltest /domain_trusts
powershell ([System.DirectoryServices.ActiveDirectory.Domain]::GetCurrentDomain()).GetAllTrustRelationships()
powershell ([System.DirectoryServices.ActiveDirectory.Forest]::GetCurrentForest()).GetAllTrustRelationships()
```

## AV ON PC

```
WMIC /Namespace:\\root\SecurityCenter2 Path AntiVirusProduct Get displayName,productState /Format:List
```

## OPTIONAL COMMANDS

```
set
systeminfo
```

## BAT FOR CHECK ALL INFO AND WRITE TO FILE:

```
@echo off

REM Here i need set file name or may be path to file: C:\ProgramData\ci.txt
set fileName=ci.txt

REM START CHECKING LOGIC

echo TOTAL SERVERS CHECK PS SCRIPT > %fileName% 2>&1
echo - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - >> %fileName% 2>&1
powershell -c "$i=0;$D=[System.DirectoryServices.ActiveDirectory.Domain]::GetCurrentDomain();$L='LDAP://'.$D;$D = [ADSI]$L;$Date = $((Get-Date).AddDays(-90).ToFileTime());$str = '(&(objectcategory=computer)(operatingSystem=*serv*)(|(lastlogon>='+$Date+')(lastlogontimestamp>='+$Date+')))';$s = [adsisearcher]$str;$s.searchRoot = $L.$D.distinguishedName;$s.PropertiesToLoad.Add('cn') > $Null;$s.PropertiesToLoad.Add('operatingsystem') > $Null;$s.PropertiesToLoad.Add('description') > $Null;$s.PropertiesToLoad.Add('distinguishedName') > $Null;Foreach ($CA in $s.FindAll()){;Write-Host $CA.Properties.Item('cn'); $CA.Properties.Item('operatingsystem'); $CA.Properties.Item('description'); $CA.Properties.Item('distinguishedName'); $i++;}; Write-host Total servers: $i" >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo. >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo TOTAL COMPUTERS CHECK PS SCRIPT >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - >> %fileName% 2>&1
powershell -c "$D=[System.DirectoryServices.ActiveDirectory.Domain]::GetCurrentDomain();$L='LDAP://'.$D;$D = [ADSI]$L;$Date = $((Get-Date).AddDays(-90).ToFileTime());$str = '(&(objectcategory=computer)(|(lastlogon>='+$Date+')(lastlogontimestamp>='+$Date+')))';$s = [adsisearcher]$str;$s.searchRoot = $L.$D.distinguishedName;$s.PageSize = 10000;$s.PropertiesToLoad.Add('cn') > $Null;Foreach ($CA in $s.FindAll()){;$i++;}; Write-Output Total computers: $i" >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo. >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo DOMAIN TRUSTS CHECK nltest /domain_trusts >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - >> %fileName% 2>&1
nltest /domain_trusts >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo. >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo DOMAIN TRUSTS CHECK GetCurrentDomain >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - >> %fileName% 2>&1
powershell ([System.DirectoryServices.ActiveDirectory.Domain]::GetCurrentDomain()).GetAllTrustRelationships() >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo. >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo DOMAIN TRUSTS CHECK GetCurrentForest >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - >> %fileName% 2>&1
powershell ([System.DirectoryServices.ActiveDirectory.Forest]::GetCurrentForest()).GetAllTrustRelationships() >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo. >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo CHECK AV >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - >> %fileName% 2>&1
WMIC /Namespace:\\root\SecurityCenter2 Path AntiVirusProduct Get displayName,productState /Format:List >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo. >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo CHECK CMD ENVIRONMENT >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - >> %fileName% 2>&1
set >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo. >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo GET SYSTEMINFO >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - >> %fileName% 2>&1
systeminfo >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - >> %fileName% 2>&1
echo. >> %fileName% 2>&1
```

## TOTAL SERVERS

```
powershell -c "$i=0;$D=[System.DirectoryServices.ActiveDirectory.Domain]::GetCurrentDomain();$L='LDAP://'.$D;$D = [ADSI]$L;$Date = $((Get-Date).AddDays(-90).ToFileTime());$str = '(&(objectcategory=computer)(operatingSystem=*serv*)(|(lastlogon>='+$Date+')(lastlogontimestamp>='+$Date+')))';$s = [adsisearcher]$str;$s.searchRoot = $L.$D.distinguishedName;$s.PropertiesToLoad.Add('cn') > $Null;$s.PropertiesToLoad.Add('operatingsystem') > $Null;$s.PropertiesToLoad.Add('description') > $Null;$s.PropertiesToLoad.Add('distinguishedName') > $Null;Foreach ($CA in $s.FindAll()){;Write-Host $CA.Properties.Item('cn'); $CA.Properties.Item('operatingsystem'); $CA.Properties.Item('description'); $CA.Properties.Item('distinguishedName'); $i++;}; Write-host Total servers: $i"
```

## TOTAL COMPUTERS

```
powershell -c "$D=[System.DirectoryServices.ActiveDirectory.Domain]::GetCurrentDomain();$L='LDAP://'.$D;$D = [ADSI]$L;$Date = $((Get-Date).AddDays(-90).ToFileTime());$str = '(&(objectcategory=computer)(|(lastlogon>='+$Date+')(lastlogontimestamp>='+$Date+')))';$s = [adsisearcher]$str;$s.searchRoot = $L.$D.distinguishedName;$s.PageSize = 10000;$s.PropertiesToLoad.Add('cn') > $Null;Foreach ($CA in $s.FindAll()){;$i++;}; Write-Output Total computers: $i"
```

powershell ([System.DirectoryServices.ActiveDirectory.Forest]::GetCurrentForest()).GetAllTrustRelationships()
